Contents

Example code for pulling data from OSDR. Documentation for the OSDR API: https://genelab.nasa.gov/genelabAPIs Useful tutorial on API json response parsing in Python: https://dataquest.io/blog/python-api-tutorial/

import requests
import json
import pandas as pd
pd.set_option('display.max_rows', None)

Let’s pull data fro GLDS-37 as an example.

# Get all files for OSD-37
response = requests.get('https://osdr.nasa.gov/genelab/data/glds/files/37').json()
